### Thread 72: 2. Key Technical Concepts
- **Lines:** 32224-32311
- **Word Count:** 458
- **Keywords:** 0, 1, 100, 152, 2
- **Breakthroughs:** 1
  - "Key Technical Concepts

- **Hybrid Architecture**: Dual-flow system where simple conversations use current ingest (unchanged), complex conversations trigger secondary multi-pass extraction
- **Classification Algorithm**: Automated detection of conversation complexity based on word count (>5k), topic shifts (‚â•3), breakthrough moments, structural analysis
- **Multi-Pass Learning Extraction**: 5-pass system (Segmentation, Connection Mapping, Per-Thread Learning, Cross-Thread Insights, Thinking Pattern Analysis)
- **Knowledge Lake API**: Flask/Python API with PostgreSQL persistence and mem0 semantic indexing, deployed on Railway
- **MCP (Model Context Protocol)**: Server protocol for AI agents to interact with external systems (stdio for Claude/CC, HTTP/SSE for Jan)
- **PostgreSQL on Railway**: Current database choice (not Supabase) due to existing setup and convenience
- **Conversation Classification**: 
  - Simple: <5k words, <3 topic shifts, linear structure
  - Complex: >5k words, ‚â•3 topic shifts, associative/web-like, breakthrough moments
  - Manual Review: 30-70 complexity score (gray zone)
- **AAE Council**: Multi-agent system (Claude GUI, Claude Code, Fred, Gemini, Jan, Manus, etc"

- **Audio**: MP3 (audio/mpeg), WAV (audio/wav), MP4 audio (audio/mp4)
- **Video**: MP4 (video/mp4)
- **PDF**: application/pdf

**Thread 72:** Breakthrough in 2. Key Technical Concepts
- Details: Key Technical Concepts

- **Hybrid Architecture**: Dual-flow system where simple conversations use current ingest (unchanged), complex conversations trigger secondary multi-pass extraction
- **Classification Algorithm**: Automated detection of conversation complexity based on word count (>5k), topic shifts (‚â•3), breakthrough moments, structural analysis
- **Multi-Pass Learning Extraction**: 5-pass system (Segmentation, Connection Mapping, Per-Thread Learning, Cross-Thread Insights, Thinking Pattern Analysis)
- **Knowledge Lake API**: Flask/Python API with PostgreSQL persistence and mem0 semantic indexing, deployed on Railway
- **MCP (Model Context Protocol)**: Server protocol for AI agents to interact with external systems (stdio for Claude/CC, HTTP/SSE for Jan)
- **PostgreSQL on Railway**: Current database choice (not Supabase) due to existing setup and convenience
- **Conversation Classification**: 
  - Simple: <5k words, <3 topic shifts, linear structure
  - Complex: >5k words, ‚â•3 topic shifts, associative/web-like, breakthrough moments
  - Manual Review: 30-70 complexity score (gray zone)
- **AAE Council**: Multi-agent system (Claude GUI, Claude Code, Fred, Gemini, Jan, Manus, etc
